   /* Add your JavaScript code here.*/ 
console.log('custom js (plugin) loaded');
	jQuery('#sign-up-submit').on('click',function(){
		console.log('sign up submitted');
		var uname = jQuery('#reg_username').val;
		var uemail = jQuery('#reg_email').val;
		var upass = jQuery('#reg_password').val;
		var data = {
			'uname' :uname,
			'upass' : upass,
			'uemail': uemail,
			'action' : 'register_user'
		}
		console.log(data);
		jQuery.ajax({
			method: 'POST',
			url: wp_params.ajaxurl,
			data: data,
			
			beforeSend: function(){
				console.log('sending registeration data');
				jQuery('.sign-up-status').html('Please wait. Processing...');
			},
			success: function(data){
			    console.log('in success for ajax');
				console.log(data);
				jQuery('.sign-up-status').html(data);	return false;
			}

		});
	});
  </script>
